Tests/Backroom/add_diskspace_to_account.html
add_diskspace_to_account
setTimeout 60000
assertTextPresent Account Details -  ${acctid}

clickAndWait link=Disk Space Used
storeSelectOptions //select[@name='${additional_disk_space_selectlist}'] avail_disk_space_options
storeGlobal javascript{ storedVars['avail_disk_space_options'][Math.floor(Math.random()*storedVars['avail_disk_space_options'].length)] } add_diskspace_amt
storeGlobal javascript{ var tmp_new_size = storedVars['add_diskspace_amt'];   while( globalStoredVars['mb_size'] == tmp_new_size){ var tmp_new_size = storedVars['avail_disk_space_options'][Math.floor(Math.random()*storedVars['avail_disk_space_options'].length)];  }  tmp_new_size } change_diskspace_amt
echo ${avail_disk_space_options} 0,25,50,75,100,125,150,175,200,225,250,275,350,300,325,375,400,450,425,475,500,525,550,575,600
echo add_diskspace_amt: ${add_diskspace_amt} add_diskspace_amt: 300
echo change_diskspace_amt: ${change_diskspace_amt} change_diskspace_amt: 425
select ${additional_disk_space_selectlist} label=${add_diskspace_amt}
assertElementPresent //input[@name='button' and @value='Continue' and @type='submit']
clickAndWait //input[@name='button' and @value='Continue' and @type='submit']
verifyElementPresent //input[@name='button' and @value='Cancel Order' and @type='submit']
assertElementPresent //input[@name='button' and @value='Finish' and @type='submit']
clickAndWait //input[@name='button' and @value='Finish' and @type='submit']
assertTextPresent ${completion_message}

check document.forms[0].elements[1]
check document.forms[0].elements[2]
check document.forms[0].elements[3]
check document.forms[0].elements[4]
check document.forms[0].elements[5]
check document.forms[0].elements[6]
check document.forms[0].elements[7]
check document.forms[0].elements[8]
check document.forms[0].elements[9]

clickAndWait edit

assertValue document.forms[0].elements[2] 127.0.0.1
assertValue document.forms[0].elements[0] localhost
